{

}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]

{

  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]

  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{

  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;

    score := m;

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]); // from non-negativity of terms
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m; // because a[k-1] <= m
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{

  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]

  // Sum(t) = Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1] = Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]

  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // this follows from the invariant of Sum
  assert t == s[..i] + [s[i]];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

```dafny
ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]); // this holds by the definition of Sum
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0; // Sum of empty sequence is 0
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1]; // by SumAppend
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m; // from induction hypothesis
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m; // add 0 <= a[k-1] <= m
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}
```

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

{

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)

  var i := 0;

    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]; // use recursion definition
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1)*m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1)*m + m;
    assert (k-1)*m + m == k*m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k*m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

  decreases |a|

  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]

  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  // The following lemma is standard and holds by definition of Sum.
  // We use a short proof by induction on the length of s.
  if i == 0 {
    assert s[..1] == [s[0]];
    assert Sum(s[..1]) == Sum([]) + s[0]; // Sum([])=0
  } else {
    SumAppend(s, i - 1);
    assert s[..i] == s[..i-1] + [s[i-1]];
    assert Sum(s[..i]) == Sum(s[..i-1]) + s[i-1];
    assert s[..i+1] == (s[..i-1] + [s[i-1]]) + [s[i]];
    assert s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]];
    assert Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
  }
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) >= 0; // since Sum(a[..k-1]) >= 0 and a[k-1] >= 0
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{

  requires 0 <= i < |s|

  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]

  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];

  decreases k

--- LLM RESPONSE (785 tokens, 7.49s) ---

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);  // use property of Sum for prefix
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]); // from induction hypothesis
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m; // from induction hypothesis
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(t[..|t|-1]) + t[|t|-1];
  assert Sum(t[..|t|-1]) == Sum(s[..i]);
  assert t[|t|-1] == s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= k * m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

// A score v is achievable for student 0 if there exists a reassignment
// b[0..n-1] with b[0] = v, all b[i] in [0, m], and Sum(b) == Sum(a).
// This holds iff v is in [0, m] and the remaining sum Sum(a) - v can be
// distributed among |a| - 1 students each scoring in [0, m].
ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  // Proof by induction on the length of the prefix
  // The lemma is used only for the last element of the prefix, so
  // we can reason about the definition of Sum.
  assert s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]];
  assert Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)

    i := i + 1;

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(a: seq<int>): int
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0 else Sum(a[..|a|-1]) + a[|a|-1]
}

ghost predicate ValidScores(a: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  forall i | 0 <= i < |a| :: 0 <= a[i] <= m
}

ghost predicate Achievable(a: seq<int>, m: int, v: int)
  requires |a| > 0
{
  0 <= v <= m &&
  Sum(a) - v >= 0 &&
  Sum(a) - v <= (|a| - 1) * m
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, i: int)
  requires 0 <= i < |s|
  ensures s[..i+1] == s[..i] + [s[i]]
  ensures Sum(s[..i+1]) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i]
{
  var t := s[..i+1];
  assert t[..|t|-1] == s[..i];
  assert t == s[..i] + [s[i]];
  assert Sum(t) == Sum(s[..i]) + s[i];
}

lemma SumBounds(a: seq<int>, m: int, k: int)
  requires 0 <= k <= |a|
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 {
    assert a[..0] == [];
    assert Sum(a[..0]) == 0;
    assert 0 <= 0 <= 0 * m;
  } else {
    SumBounds(a, m, k - 1);
    SumAppend(a, k - 1);
    assert 0 <= a[k-1] <= m;
    assert Sum(a[..k]) == Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) <= (k-1) * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1];
    assert Sum(a[..k-1]) + a[k-1] <= (k-1) * m + m;
    assert (k-1) * m + m == k * m;
    assert 0 <= Sum(a[..k]) <= k * m;
  }
}

method GradeAllocation(a: seq<int>, m: int) returns (score: int)
  requires |a| > 0
  requires m >= 0
  requires ValidScores(a, m)
  ensures Achievable(a, m, score)
  ensures forall v | score < v <= m :: !Achievable(a, m, v)
{
  var s := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant s == Sum(a[..i])
  {
    SumAppend(a, i);
    s := s + a[i];
    i := i + 1;
  }

  SumBounds(a, m, |a|);
  if s < m {
    score := s;
  } else {
    score := m;
  }
}
